<script>
    (function() {


        window.logRocketSetupComplete = false;

        window.logRocketSetup = function(userId, email, membership) {
            if (!window.LogRocket) return;
            LogRocket.identify(userId, { email: email, membership: membership});
            logRocketSetupComplete = true;
            return logRocketSetupComplete;
        }


        var app = angular.module('lnApp',
        [
            
            'ngSanitize',
            'ngLocale',
            'ngAnimate',
            'ngMessages',
            'ngCookies',
            
            'csgp.config',
            'csgp.feature',
            'csgp.pubsub',
            'csgp.api',
            'csgp.body',
            'csgp.viewdata',
            
            'ln.search.map_and_placards'
        ]);
        log.logLevelSetup('error', 'error', '/services/log');

        app.constant('log', log);


app.config(function ($locationProvider, $provide,$compileProvider) {
    $compileProvider.aHrefSanitizationWhitelist(/^\s*(https?|ftp|mailto|file|intent|lndlapp):/);
    if (history.pushState) {
        $locationProvider.html5Mode(true);
    }
    $provide.decorator("$exceptionHandler", ['$delegate', 'log', function ($delegate, log) {
        return function (exception, cause) {
            $delegate(exception, cause);
            exception.message += ' (caused by "' + cause + '")';
            log.error('General UI error occured: ' + exception.message);
        };
    }]);
});


app.config(function ($httpProvider, $compileProvider) {
    $compileProvider.aHrefSanitizationWhitelist(/^\s*(https?|ftp|mailto|file|intent|lndlapp):/);
    $httpProvider.interceptors.push(function () {
        return {
            'request': function (config) {

                if (config.url && config.url.indexOf('/services/') === 0 && !config.wrapped) {
                    throw new Error('Calling "' + config.url + '" every AJAX service call must use the Api service module instead of $http directly.');
                }
                return config;
            }
        };
    });
});
